uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _DarkCorner;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainHighLightOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SSSColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Frequency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Amplitude;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WaveLength;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Power;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BrightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DarkColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighBlend;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BaseColor_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MaxShadow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _LightPow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _LightOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _WindDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindRang;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindSpeed;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindNoise;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD12;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec4 u_xlat4;
vec4 u_xlat5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xy = in_POSITION0.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xz;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xz * in_POSITION0.xx + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xz * in_POSITION0.zz + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _WaveLength;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _Time.yyy * _Frequency.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed));
    u_xlat8.xyz = fract(u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz + in_COLOR0.zzz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(6.28000021, 6.28000021, 6.28000021);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed)) + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = sin(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _Amplitude.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * in_COLOR0.www;
    u_xlat24 = min(abs(in_POSITION0.y), 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = log2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat24 * _Power;
    u_xlat24 = exp2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat24) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = sqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat0.w = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.5 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat8.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].z + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].x;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindNoise;
    u_xlat8.x = _Time.y * _WindSpeed + u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat8.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.200000003;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindRang;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.w * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat1.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat2.x = cos(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].zxy * _WindDir.yyy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].zxy * _WindDir.xxx + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].zxy * _WindDir.zzz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat10.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat8.xxxx * u_xlat9.yyxz;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat3.xw * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat5.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat6.w = u_xlat3.z * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + (-u_xlat10.y);
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat3.zy * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat10.zx;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat5.yzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.w = u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat3.yz * u_xlat9.zy + (-u_xlat10.xz);
    u_xlat6.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat10.y;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat6.ywz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.z = u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xwz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_31) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat3.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat3.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_15)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_7.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_7.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat24 = min(max(u_xlat24, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat24 = clamp(u_xlat24, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD12.z = u_xlat24;
    u_xlat24 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	mediump vec4 _GISpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _ExposureColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SSSColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Frequency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _Amplitude;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WaveLength;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Power;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BrightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DarkColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighBlend;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _HighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BaseColor_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MaxShadow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _LightPow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _LightOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _WindDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindRang;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindSpeed;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _WindNoise;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD12;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat14;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8 = min(max(u_xlat8, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8 = clamp(u_xlat8, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat8) * u_xlat8 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_19 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat4.zxy * u_xlat5.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat5.zxy + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.z = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat5.z = min(max(u_xlat5.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat5.z = clamp(u_xlat5.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat21) + 1.0;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat5.z + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat8 = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat8 = float(1.0) / u_xlat8;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat21 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat5.y = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat8 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat8 = clamp(u_xlat8, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat8) * u_xlat8 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_19 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8 = min(max(u_xlat8, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8 = clamp(u_xlat8, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat8) * u_xlat8 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_19 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat14;

    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8.x = min(max(u_xlat8.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8.x = clamp(u_xlat8.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * u_xlat8.xxxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;

    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat8 = min(max(u_xlat8, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat8 = clamp(u_xlat8, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat3.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat3.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat8) * u_xlat8 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_19 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_19) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_16 = _RoughNessOffset;

    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_16;

    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat7;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD12.xxx * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_16) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);

    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD12.z = u_xlat18;
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    return;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-u_xlat10_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_10 = log2(vs_TEXCOORD12.z);
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_10 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat16_10 = exp2(u_xlat16_10);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat10_0.xyz;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _WaveLength;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _Time.yyy * _Frequency.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed));
    u_xlat8.xyz = fract(u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz + in_COLOR0.zzz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(6.28000021, 6.28000021, 6.28000021);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed)) + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = sin(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _Amplitude.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * in_COLOR0.www;
    u_xlat24 = min(abs(in_POSITION0.y), 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = log2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat24 * _Power;
    u_xlat24 = exp2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat24) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = sqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat0.w = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.5 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat8.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].z + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].x;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindNoise;
    u_xlat8.x = _Time.y * _WindSpeed + u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat8.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.200000003;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindRang;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.w * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat1.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat2.x = cos(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].zxy * _WindDir.yyy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].zxy * _WindDir.xxx + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].zxy * _WindDir.zzz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat10.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat8.xxxx * u_xlat9.yyxz;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat3.xw * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat5.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat6.w = u_xlat3.z * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + (-u_xlat10.y);
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat3.zy * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat10.zx;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat5.yzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.w = u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;

    u_xlat6.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat10.y;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat6.ywz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.z = u_xlat6.x;

    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);

    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);

    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;

vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_POSITION0.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xz;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xz * in_POSITION0.xx + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xz * in_POSITION0.zz + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _WaveLength;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _Time.yyy * _Frequency.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed));
    u_xlat8.xyz = fract(u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz + in_COLOR0.zzz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(6.28000021, 6.28000021, 6.28000021);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed)) + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = sin(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _Amplitude.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * in_COLOR0.www;
    u_xlat24 = min(abs(in_POSITION0.y), 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = log2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat24 * _Power;
    u_xlat24 = exp2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat24) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = sqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat0.w = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.5 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat8.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].z + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].x;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindNoise;
    u_xlat8.x = _Time.y * _WindSpeed + u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat8.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.200000003;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindRang;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.w * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat1.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat2.x = cos(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].zxy * _WindDir.yyy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].zxy * _WindDir.xxx + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].zxy * _WindDir.zzz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat10.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat8.xxxx * u_xlat9.yyxz;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat3.xw * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat5.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat6.w = u_xlat3.z * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + (-u_xlat10.y);
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat3.zy * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat10.zx;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat5.yzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.w = u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat3.yz * u_xlat9.zy + (-u_xlat10.xz);
    u_xlat6.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat10.y;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat6.ywz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.z = u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xwz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_31) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat3.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat3.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_15)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_7.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_7.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat24 = min(max(u_xlat24, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat24 = clamp(u_xlat24, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD12.z = u_xlat24;
    u_xlat24 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

{

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);

    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16) * u_xlat16 + 1.0;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;

vec4 u_xlat0;

vec3 u_xlat4;

vec3 u_xlat6;
float u_xlat8;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat21;
mediump float u_xlat16_24;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_24 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_24);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_24) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat4.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat4.zxy * u_xlat5.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat5.zxy + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.z = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = clamp(u_xlat5.z, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat21) + 1.0;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat5.z + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat8 = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat8 = float(1.0) / u_xlat8;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat21 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat5.y = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz);

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat2.xzw, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xzw, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_25 * u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16_25 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_6.x;

    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD12.xxx * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat4.zxy * u_xlat5.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat5.zxy + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.z = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat5.z = min(max(u_xlat5.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat5.z = clamp(u_xlat5.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat21) + 1.0;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * u_xlat21;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat5.z + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat8 = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat8 = float(1.0) / u_xlat8;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat8 * u_xlat1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat21 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat5.y = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat9 = vs_TEXCOORD6.y * u_xlat2.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = max(u_xlat9, -0.5);
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat9 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat2.xzw, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9 = min(max(u_xlat9, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xzw, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_25 = min(max(u_xlat16_25, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_25 * u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16_25 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat9;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD12.xxx * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

vec3 u_xlat3;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
float u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
float u_xlat16;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat10_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.5);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16 = clamp(u_xlat16, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16) * u_xlat16 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat9;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);

    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.5);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9 = min(max(u_xlat9, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16 = min(max(u_xlat16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16 = clamp(u_xlat16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + vec3(u_xlat16_22);

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16) * u_xlat16 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat9;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;

    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;

    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;

    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainColor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;

};

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;

out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD12;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_21) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xz / _BaseColor_ST.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy + _BaseColor_ST.zw;
    u_xlat1.z = u_xlat0.y + _HighOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseColor;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD12;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump float u_xlat16_13;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD12.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13 = log2(vs_TEXCOORD12.z);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * _HighBlend;
    u_xlat16_13 = exp2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_13) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_13;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    return;
}

#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
attribute highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;

vec4 u_xlat0;

vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_POSITION0.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xz;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xz * in_POSITION0.xx + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xz * in_POSITION0.zz + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _WaveLength;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _Time.yyy * _Frequency.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed));
    u_xlat8.xyz = fract(u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz + in_COLOR0.zzz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(6.28000021, 6.28000021, 6.28000021);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vec3(vec3(_WindSpeed, _WindSpeed, _WindSpeed)) + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = sin(u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _Amplitude.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * in_COLOR0.www;
    u_xlat24 = min(abs(in_POSITION0.y), 1.0);
    u_xlat24 = log2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat24 * _Power;
    u_xlat24 = exp2(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat24) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = sqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat0.w = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.5 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat8.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].z + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].x;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindNoise;
    u_xlat8.x = _Time.y * _WindSpeed + u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat8.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.200000003;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * _WindRang;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.w * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat1.x = sin(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat2.x = cos(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].zxy * _WindDir.yyy;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].zxy * _WindDir.xxx + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].zxy * _WindDir.zzz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat10.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat10.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat8.xxxx * u_xlat9.yyxz;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat3.xw * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat5.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat6.w = u_xlat3.z * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + (-u_xlat10.y);
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat3.zy * u_xlat9.yz + u_xlat10.zx;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat5.yzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.w = u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat3.yz * u_xlat9.zy + (-u_xlat10.xz);
    u_xlat6.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat10.y;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat6.ywz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.z = u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xwz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_31) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);

    u_xlat3.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;

    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_7.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_7.z;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;

    u_xlat4.w = u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat3.yz * u_xlat9.zy + (-u_xlat10.xz);
    u_xlat6.z = u_xlat3.w * u_xlat9.x + u_xlat10.y;
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat6.ywz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat4.z = u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xwz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat24 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat3.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    u_xlat24 = max(u_xlat24, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat24 = inversesqrt(u_xlat24);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;

    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat24) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    vs_TEXCOORD12.xy = vec2(0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat4.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;

    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;

    u_xlat4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;

    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;

    u_xlat3 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.y * _HightMul + _HightOffset;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat3 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat3.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
    u_xlat7 = clamp(u_xlat7, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_Position = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat7);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;

    u_xlat14 = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;

    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat7 * u_xlat7;
