    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3 = u_xlat3 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat3.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7 = min(max(u_xlat7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7 = clamp(u_xlat7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxxx * vec4(u_xlat7);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.z = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat1.z + (-_LightPow);
    u_xlat14 = (-_LightPow) + _LightOffset;
    u_xlat14 = float(1.0) / u_xlat14;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat14 * u_xlat7;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7 = min(max(u_xlat7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7 = clamp(u_xlat7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.z = u_xlat7 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat7 * u_xlat7;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * u_xlat0.xz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat1.y = in_POSITION0.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat9 = vs_TEXCOORD6.y * u_xlat2.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.xzw = u_xlat2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = max(u_xlat9, -0.5);
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat9 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);

    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;

#else

#endif

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3

#else

#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_25 * u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16_25 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat9;

    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD12.xxx * _RimColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);

    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_5.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.5);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16 = clamp(u_xlat16, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat6.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16) * u_xlat16 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat9;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat10_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.02250004, 1.02250004, 1.02250004);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_1.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif

    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;

    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_5.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_5.y * u_xlat16_1.x + (-vs_TEXCOORD6.y);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, -0.5);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9 = min(max(u_xlat9, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9 = clamp(u_xlat9, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16 = min(max(u_xlat16, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16 = clamp(u_xlat16, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_22 = max(u_xlat16_22, _MaxShadow);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + vec3(u_xlat16_22);

    u_xlat6.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat6.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat9) + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16) * u_xlat16 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16 + u_xlat2.x;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD12.zzz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _SSSColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_0.w * 2.0 + -1.0;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _MainColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD12.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_HighColor, _HighColor, _HighColor)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-u_xlat16_0.xyz);

    u_xlat16_13 = exp2(u_xlat16_13);

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_9 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xzw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_9)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xzw;

    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat4.zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat4.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat1.xz / _BaseColor_ST.xy;
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat2.xy + _BaseColor_ST.zw;
    u_xlat2.z = u_xlat1.y + _HighOffset;
    u_xlat2.z = clamp(u_xlat2.z, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD12.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz + (-u_xlat10_0.xyz);

    u_xlat16_13 = exp2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_13) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat10_0.xyz;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;

}

 Pass {
  Name "ShadowCaster"
  LOD 300
  Tags { "IGNOREPROJECTOR" = "true" "LIGHTMODE" = "SHADOWCASTER" "QUEUE" = "Geometry+400" "RenderPipeline" = "LightweightPipeline" "RenderType" = "Transparent" }

  GpuProgramID 92996
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 7e1f6e5f7ab0171f
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
#define SV_TARGET0 gl_FragData[0]
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GlobalLightEmiss;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MaskColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MaskColor2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MaskFlip;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_0 + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}
